  Fontconfig configuration is done via /etc/fonts/conf.avail and conf.d.

  msgid_bugs_address='http://bugzilla.gnome.org/'; \

  msgid_bugs_address='http://bugzilla.gnome.org/enter_bug.cgi?product=GStreamer'; \

  '' | 0.[0-9] | 0.[0-9].* | 0.1[0-5] | 0.1[0-5].* | 0.16 | 0.16.[0-1]*) \

      --files-from=./POTFILES.in \
      --copyright-holder='' \
      --msgid-bugs-address="$msgid_bugs_address" \
    ;; \
  *) \
    /usr/bin/xgettext --default-domain=gst-plugins-base-0.10 --directory=.. \
      --add-comments=TRANSLATORS: --keyword=_ --keyword=N_  \
      --files-from=./POTFILES.in \
      --copyright-holder='' \
      --package-name="${package_gnu}gst-plugins-base" \
      --package-version='0.10.36' \
      --msgid-bugs-address="$msgid_bugs_address" \
    ;; \
esac

      mv gst-plugins-base-0.10.po ./gst-plugins-base-0.10.pot; \
    fi; \
  else \
    mv gst-plugins-base-0.10.po ./gst-plugins-base-0.10.pot; \
  fi; \
